***энциклопедия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:энциклопедия.html>энциклопе́дия</a> (7570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">encyclopaedia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">general education</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Renaissance <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐγκυκλοπαιδεία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">enkuklopaideía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">education in the circle of arts and sciences</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a mistaken univerbated form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Koine_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Koine Greek">Koine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐγκύκλιος παιδείᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">enkúklios paideíā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">education in the circle of arts and sciences</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐγκύκλιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">enkúklios</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">circular</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παιδείᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paideíā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">child-rearing, education</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эпидермис.html>эпиде́рмис</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">epidɛ́rmis</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эпидермис.html>эпиде́рмиса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эпидермис.html>эпиде́рмисы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эпидермис.html>эпиде́рмисов</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> epidermis</li></ol>

</p>
